Supplementary data 2 of Hayakawa et al. (2020, Astrophysical Journal, DOI: 10.3847/1538-4357/ab65c9) 'Thaddäus Derfflinger’s sunspot observations during 1802-1824: A primary reference to understand the Dalton Minimum'. The sunspot positions have been extracted mainly from his summary manuscript and supplemented with his logbooks. The original manuscripts are preserved in Kremsmünster Observatory.


Cols  Meaning
------------------------------------------------------------------
 1- 4 Year
 6- 7 Month
 9-10 Day (Gregorian)
12-16 Hours and minutes: clock readings or manually adjusted clock
      readings (see below). If manually adjusted, the grid images
      still contain the original clock reading in the filename.
18-27 Julian day
29-33 Position angle clockwise (North = 0, pole turned to the west 
      is > 0, pole turned to the east < 0), in degrees
37-40 Error in position angle. For types T and M (see below), it is
      set to 10 degrees, for type R and r, it is the 68% confidence
      interval of the posterior distribution of the position angle.
42-46 Heliographic central meridian distance ('relative longitude')
50-53 Uncertainty of the central meridian distance resulting from 
      the uncertainty of the position angle or from the confidence
      intervals of the posterior distributions of the rotational
      matching.
55-59 Heliographic latitude in degrees
63-66 Uncertainty of the latitude resulting from the uncertainty of
      the position angle or from the confidence intervals of the
      posterior distributions of the rotational matching.
68-68 Type of observation:
      T  -  the time of day is used, for which the observation is 
            drawn in the logbooks (clock reading)
      M  -  manually adjusted observing time to match a sequence 
            of days. Only obvious outliers were corrected.
      R  -  rotational matching of a sequence of days. The times of
            the observations have no meaning any longer.
      r  -  also rotational matching, but these spots did not take 
            part in the matching. They were measured after the 
            matching had fixed the position angle.
70-   This field gives the clock corrections applied to the times
      in columns 12-16 to obtain the position angle of the Sun. A
      negative value means the true mean local time was smaller
      than the clock reading in columns 12-16.
------------------------------------------------------------------
